U lipnja 1968 izdanje Scientific American, Martin Gardner opisao u svojoj \"Matematičke igre\" stup igre po CL Baker koja je slična FreeCell, osim što su kartice na miljea izgradio odijelu nego po alternativnim bojama. Gardner je napisao: \"Igra je učio Baker je njegov otac, koji je pak to naučio od Engleza tijekom 1920-ih.\" Ova varijanta se sada zove Baker igra. FreeCell je porijeklo može sežu još do 1945. godine, a skandinavski igra zove Napoleona u St. Heleni (ne igra Napoleona u St. Helena, također poznat kao četrdeset Lopovi).\r\n\r\nPavao Alfille promijenio Baker igra čineći kartice graditi u skladu s alternativnim bojama, stvarajući FreeCell. On provodi prvi računalni inačicu u TUTOR programski jezik za PLATO obrazovni računalni sustav u 1978. Alfille bio u mogućnosti prikazati lako prepoznatljive grafičke slike kartaju na 512 * 512 crno-bijeli zaslon na PLATO sustava.\r\n\r\nOvaj izvorni FreeCell okruženju dopušteno igre sa 4C10 stupovima i 1C10 stanica Osim standardnog 8 * 4 igre. Za svaku varijantu, program pohranjuje popis rangirani od igrača s najdužim dobitku tragove. Tu je i sustav za turnir koji dopustio ljudima da se natječu za osvajanje teško ručno ubrano ponude. Pavao Alfille opisuje ranu FreeCell okoliš detaljnije u intervjuu od 2000.\r\n\r\n\r\nSolver složenosti\r\nFreeCell Igra ima stalan broj kartica. To znači da je u stalnom vremenu, osoba ili računalo moglo navesti sve moguće poteze iz određenog početnu konfiguraciju i otkriti dobitnu skup poteza ili, pod pretpostavkom da igra ne može riješiti, nedostatak istih. Za izvođenje zanimljivu analizu složenosti mora konstruirati generalizirani verziju FreeCell igra sa 4 * n karticama. Ova generalizirana verzija igre je NP-potpun; malo je vjerojatno da bilo koji algoritam učinkovitiji od potrage brutalni postoji koji može naći rješenja za proizvoljne generalizirane FreeCell konfiguracije.\r\n\r\nPostoje 52! To view the Paytable, click the i-button in the keypad, alternatively see the Payout section below.\r\n\r\nHow to Play\r\n\r\nSelect a chip value, place your bets, spin the wheel, and wait to see if you have correctly predicted the winning number.\r\n\r\n- Selecting a chip value. To select the desired chip value, click a chip in the keypad area. If there are active arrows to the left and right of the chips, click these to see additional chip values.\r\n- You can point at different positions of the table to highlight the bets. When a bet position is highlighted, a window appears and displays the minimum and maximum bet limits for that bet.\r\n- Placing one or several bets. To place a bet, select the chip value and click either a number or a betting position on the table. Additional clicks add the required number of chips of the same value to the selected bet area.\r\n- After a bet is placed, you can point at the chips on the table to view the total value of the bet and the total payout if the bet wins.\r\n- Spinning the wheel. When you have finished betting, click the spin button to start a game round. The ball is then launched into the roulette wheel. The amount you bet is deducted from your account. The ball lands in a slot and the number on the slot is the winning number.\r\n- A player can stop the roulette wheel anytime while it is spinning, by clicking the spin button. This function is not available during Autoplay (not available in all casinos).\r\n- It is possible to spin the wheel without placing any bets (not available in all casinos).  \r\n- Checking the winning number. When the ball lands in a slot, the winning number is announced and all winning bets are paid. The winning number is displayed on the roulette wheel. Your winnings are also displayed in the game panel and are added to your Cash amount. All losing bets are cleared from the table.\r\n- Playing again. Click the rebet button to place the same bet as in the previous round. Alternatively, click the clear all bets button to clear the table of all previous bets, place any new bets, and then click the spin button.\r\n\r\nAuto Adjust Bet\r\n\r\n- If a bet exceeds the bet limit or table limit, or if the player is out of money, the Auto Adjust Bet function automatically adjusts the bet to the highest possible amount. If the bet consists of several bet positions, it will be scaled down proportionally over the included bet positions. If the scaled down bet is too small to cover all desired bet positions, chips will be placed on as many of these positions as possible. If all desired bet positions cannot be covered, the game will randomly choose which positions should receive chips.\r\n- To activate this function, open the Game settings menu.\r\n\r\nSpecial Bets Panel\r\n\r\n- Special bets are types of call bets and are made by placing chips directly on the name of the bet in the Special bets panel.
